Grammar:
 select_stmt -> <14> IF OPENPA expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDIF
              | <15> IF OPENPA expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ELSE COLON statement ENDIF;
 equality_expr -> <34> relational_expr
                | <35> equality_expr EQ relational_expr
                | <36> equality_expr NE relational_expr;
 loop_stmt -> <16> WHILE OPENPA expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDWHILE
            | <17> DO COLON compound_stmt ENDDO OPENPA expr CLOSEPA
            | <18> FOR OPENPA opt_expr SEMICOL opt_expr SEMICOL opt_expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDFOR;
 expr -> <21> assign_expr;
 add_expr -> <42> mult_expr
           | <43> add_expr PLUS mult_expr
           | <44> add_expr SUB mult_expr;
Sprogram' -> <61> program;
 stmt_list -> <4> statement
            | <5> stmt_list statement;
 cast_expr -> <49> unary_expr
            | <50> OPENPA type CLOSEPA cast_expr;
 mult_expr -> <45> cast_expr
            | <46> mult_expr MUL cast_expr
            | <47> mult_expr DIV cast_expr
            | <48> mult_expr MOD cast_expr;
 assign_expr -> <27> conditional_expr
              | <28> unary_expr assign_op assign_expr;
 decl -> <3> ID COLON type ASSIGN conditional_expr SEMICOL;
 expr_stmt -> <12> expr SEMICOL
            | <13> SEMICOL;
 type -> <22> INT
       | <23> STR
       | <24> FLOAT
       | <25> BOOL
       | <26> CHAR;
 compound_stmt -> <1> stmt_list
                | <2> ;
 logical_and_expr -> <32> equality_expr
                   | <33> logical_and_expr AND equality_expr;
 prime_expr -> <55> ID
             | <56> NUM_CONST
             | <57> STR_CONST
             | <58> CHAR_CONST
             | <59> BOOL_CONST
             | <60> OPENPA expr CLOSEPA;
 conditional_expr -> <29> logical_or_expr;
 assign_op -> <51> ASSIGN;
 unary_op -> <52> NOT;
 opt_expr -> <19> expr
           | <20> ;
 statement -> <6> expr_stmt
            | <7> select_stmt
            | <8> loop_stmt
            | <9> decl
            | <10> per_def_func;
 unary_expr -> <53> prime_expr
             | <54> unary_op cast_expr;
 logical_or_expr -> <30> logical_and_expr
                  | <31> logical_or_expr OR logical_and_expr;
 program -> <0> STARTINPUT COLON compound_stmt ENDINPUT;
 relational_expr -> <37> add_expr
                  | <38> relational_expr LT add_expr
                  | <39> relational_expr GT add_expr
                  | <40> relational_expr GE add_expr
                  | <41> relational_expr LE add_expr;
 per_def_func -> <11> OUT OPENPA prime_expr CLOSEPA SEMICOL;

State 0:
    program' -> * program, {EOF}

State 1:
    program -> STARTINPUT * COLON compound_stmt ENDINPUT, {EOF}

State 2:
    program' -> program *, {EOF}

State 3:
    program -> STARTINPUT COLON * compound_stmt ENDINPUT, {EOF}

State 4:
    select_stmt -> IF * OPENPA expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ELSE COLON statement ENDIF, {IF, CHAR_CONST, SEMICOL, OPENPA, OUT, FOR, BOOL_CONST, DO, NOT, STR_CONST, NUM_CONST, WHILE, ID}
    select_stmt -> IF * OPENPA expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDIF, {IF, CHAR_CONST, SEMICOL, OPENPA, OUT, FOR, BOOL_CONST, DO, NOT, STR_CONST, NUM_CONST, WHILE, ID}
    select_stmt -> IF * OPENPA expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ELSE COLON statement ENDIF, {ENDINPUT}
    select_stmt -> IF * OPENPA expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDIF, {ENDINPUT}

State 5:
    statement -> select_stmt *, {IF, CHAR_CONST, SEMICOL, OPENPA, OUT, FOR, BOOL_CONST, DO, NOT, STR_CONST, NUM_CONST, WHILE, ID}
    statement -> select_stmt *, {ENDINPUT}

State 6:
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {LT}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {DIV}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {ASSIGN}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {OR}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {GE}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {GT}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {LE}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {AND}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {PLUS}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {MUL}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {SUB}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {SEMICOL}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {MOD}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {NE}
    prime_expr -> CHAR_CONST *, {EQ}

State 7:
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * NE relational_expr, {EQ}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * EQ relational_expr, {NE}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * EQ relational_expr, {SEMICOL}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * NE relational_expr, {NE}
    logical_and_expr -> equality_expr *, {SEMICOL}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * EQ relational_expr, {EQ}
    logical_and_expr -> equality_expr *, {OR}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * NE relational_expr, {AND}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * EQ relational_expr, {AND}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * NE relational_expr, {OR}
    logical_and_expr -> equality_expr *, {AND}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * NE relational_expr, {SEMICOL}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * EQ relational_expr, {OR}

State 8:
    expr_stmt -> SEMICOL *, {IF, CHAR_CONST, SEMICOL, OPENPA, OUT, FOR, BOOL_CONST, DO, NOT, STR_CONST, NUM_CONST, WHILE, ID}
    expr_stmt -> SEMICOL *, {ENDINPUT}

State 9:
    statement -> loop_stmt *, {IF, CHAR_CONST, SEMICOL, OPENPA, OUT, FOR, BOOL_CONST, DO, NOT, STR_CONST, NUM_CONST, WHILE, ID}
    statement -> loop_stmt *, {ENDINPUT}

State 10:
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {GT}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {LE}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {GE}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {SEMICOL}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {PLUS}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {GT}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {LE}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {AND}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {AND}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {NE}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {MOD}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {NE}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {MUL}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {OR}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {LT}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {SEMICOL}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {GE}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {DIV}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {MOD}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {ASSIGN}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {OR}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {LT}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {DIV}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {MUL}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {EQ}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {SUB}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {EQ}
    cast_expr -> OPENPA * type CLOSEPA cast_expr, {SUB}
    prime_expr -> OPENPA * expr CLOSEPA, {PLUS}

State 11:
    add_expr -> add_expr * PLUS mult_expr, {PLUS}
    add_expr -> add_expr * PLUS mult_expr, {SUB}
    add_expr -> add_expr * SUB mult_expr, {SUB}
    add_expr -> add_expr * SUB mult_expr, {PLUS}
    relational_expr -> add_expr *, {OR}
    relational_expr -> add_expr *, {GT}
    add_expr -> add_expr * PLUS mult_expr, {GE}
    add_expr -> add_expr * SUB mult_expr, {GE}
    add_expr -> add_expr * SUB mult_expr, {OR}
    add_expr -> add_expr * PLUS mult_expr, {OR}
    add_expr -> add_expr * SUB mult_expr, {SEMICOL}
    add_expr -> add_expr * PLUS mult_expr, {GT}
    add_expr -> add_expr * SUB mult_expr, {GT}
    add_expr -> add_expr * PLUS mult_expr, {AND}
    add_expr -> add_expr * SUB mult_expr, {AND}
    relational_expr -> add_expr *, {EQ}
    add_expr -> add_expr * PLUS mult_expr, {SEMICOL}
    add_expr -> add_expr * PLUS mult_expr, {NE}
    add_expr -> add_expr * SUB mult_expr, {NE}
    add_expr -> add_expr * SUB mult_expr, {EQ}
    relational_expr -> add_expr *, {GE}
    add_expr -> add_expr * PLUS mult_expr, {EQ}
    relational_expr -> add_expr *, {AND}
    add_expr -> add_expr * SUB mult_expr, {LT}
    relational_expr -> add_expr *, {SEMICOL}
    relational_expr -> add_expr *, {NE}
    add_expr -> add_expr * PLUS mult_expr, {LT}
    relational_expr -> add_expr *, {LE}
    relational_expr -> add_expr *, {LT}
    add_expr -> add_expr * PLUS mult_expr, {LE}
    add_expr -> add_expr * SUB mult_expr, {LE}

State 12:
    expr_stmt -> expr * SEMICOL, {IF, CHAR_CONST, SEMICOL, OPENPA, OUT, FOR, BOOL_CONST, DO, NOT, STR_CONST, NUM_CONST, WHILE, ID}
    expr_stmt -> expr * SEMICOL, {ENDINPUT}

State 13:
    loop_stmt -> FOR * OPENPA opt_expr SEMICOL opt_expr SEMICOL opt_expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDFOR, {ENDINPUT}
    loop_stmt -> FOR * OPENPA opt_expr SEMICOL opt_expr SEMICOL opt_expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDFOR, {IF, CHAR_CONST, SEMICOL, OPENPA, OUT, FOR, BOOL_CONST, DO, NOT, STR_CONST, NUM_CONST, WHILE, ID}

State 14:
    compound_stmt -> stmt_list *, {ENDINPUT}
    stmt_list -> stmt_list * statement, {IF, CHAR_CONST, SEMICOL, OPENPA, OUT, FOR, BOOL_CONST, DO, NOT, STR_CONST, NUM_CONST, WHILE, ID}
    stmt_list -> stmt_list * statement, {ENDINPUT}

State 15:
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {MOD}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {EQ}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {LT}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {PLUS}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {GE}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {DIV}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {NE}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {SUB}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {OR}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {SEMICOL}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {GT}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {LE}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {AND}
    mult_expr -> cast_expr *, {MUL}

State 16:
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {LT}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {OR}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {GT}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {LE}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {AND}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {ASSIGN}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {DIV}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {MUL}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {PLUS}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {SUB}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {SEMICOL}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {EQ}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {MOD}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {GE}
    prime_expr -> NUM_CONST *, {NE}

State 17:
    loop_stmt -> WHILE * OPENPA expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDWHILE, {ENDINPUT}
    loop_stmt -> WHILE * OPENPA expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDWHILE, {IF, CHAR_CONST, SEMICOL, OPENPA, OUT, FOR, BOOL_CONST, DO, NOT, STR_CONST, NUM_CONST, WHILE, ID}

State 18:
    add_expr -> mult_expr *, {PLUS}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MOD cast_expr, {PLUS}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {PLUS}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {GE}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MOD cast_expr, {AND}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {NE}
    add_expr -> mult_expr *, {OR}
    add_expr -> mult_expr *, {AND}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {OR}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MOD cast_expr, {MUL}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MOD cast_expr, {OR}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {SEMICOL}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {GT}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {MUL}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {AND}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {MOD}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MOD cast_expr, {LT}
    add_expr -> mult_expr *, {NE}
    add_expr -> mult_expr *, {EQ}

    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {EQ}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {LT}
    add_expr -> mult_expr *, {LT}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {DIV}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {SUB}
    add_expr -> mult_expr *, {LE}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MOD cast_expr, {SUB}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {LE}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MOD cast_expr, {LE}
    add_expr -> mult_expr *, {SUB}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {PLUS}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MOD cast_expr, {GE}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {GE}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MOD cast_expr, {NE}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {NE}
    add_expr -> mult_expr *, {GE}
    add_expr -> mult_expr *, {GT}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {MUL}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {SEMICOL}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {OR}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MOD cast_expr, {SEMICOL}

    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {AND}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MOD cast_expr, {MOD}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {MOD}
    add_expr -> mult_expr *, {SEMICOL}

    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {LT}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MOD cast_expr, {DIV}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * MUL cast_expr, {DIV}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {SUB}
    mult_expr -> mult_expr * DIV cast_expr, {LE}

State 19:
    expr -> assign_expr *, {SEMICOL}
